<h2><a aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" href="#getting-started" id="user-content-getting-started"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z" fill-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></a>Getting Started</h2>
<p>Please follow the <a href="#installation--usage">installation procedure</a> and then run the following:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-c1">__future__</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> print_function
<span class="pl-k">import</span> time
<span class="pl-k">import</span> kubernetes.client
<span class="pl-k">from</span> kubernetes.client.rest <span class="pl-k">import</span> ApiException
<span class="pl-k">from</span> pprint <span class="pl-k">import</span> pprint

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Configure API key authorization: BearerToken</span>
kubernetes.client.configuration.api_key[<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>authorization<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>] <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>YOUR_API_KEY<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Uncomment below to setup prefix (e.g. Bearer) for API key, if needed</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> kubernetes.client.configuration.api_key_prefix['authorization'] = 'Bearer'</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> create an instance of the API class</span>
api_instance <span class="pl-k">=</span> kubernetes.client.AdmissionregistrationApi()

<span class="pl-k">try</span>:
    api_response <span class="pl-k">=</span> api_instance.get_api_group()
    pprint(api_response)
<span class="pl-k">except</span> ApiException <span class="pl-k">as</span> e:
    <span class="pl-c1">print</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Exception when calling AdmissionregistrationApi-&gt;get_api_group: <span class="pl-c1">%s</span><span class="pl-cce">\n</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">%</span> e)
</pre></div>

<h2><a aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" href="#bearertoken" id="user-content-bearertoken"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z" fill-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></a>BearerToken</h2>

<li><strong>Type</strong>: API key</li>

</ul>
